<h2 class="gb-headline gb-headline-1bb9c1ea gb-headline-text">Meet Olivia</h2>



<p class="has-text-align-center has-555555-color has-text-color">Hi, I’m Olivia school assistant, food lover, and creator of Golden Era Recipes. After years of trial, error, and green sludge smoothies, I turned to the healing wisdom of my grandmother and mother to make food that’s good, grounded, and full of heart.</p>



<p class="has-text-align-center"><strong><em>“Make it with heart, and it will heal.” – Grandma Dalida</em></strong></p>
